<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:mennen.html>mennen</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*<a href = vnd.unilang:mennen.html>mennen</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Vulgar_Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Vulgar Latin">Vulgar Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">*menō</i> or <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Vulgar_Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Vulgar Latin">Vulgar Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">*minō</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">minō</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">I drive, impel</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, a <a href = vnd.unilang:rare.html>rare</a> Classical and <a href = vnd.unilang:later.html>later</a> variant of deponent <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">minor</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:mennen.html>mennen</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">literally</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> To lead (a) draught animal(s)</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> To drive a drawn vehicle (especially chariot) or plow</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> To deliver the load of such transport</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figurative</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> To take the lead, conduct, guide, command (troops), steer people/ events</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> To be engaged in any of the above senses, e.g. to have the lead, be in charge</li></ol>

***mens.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:mens.html>mens</a> (598)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_4">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">mensche</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">mennisko</i>, a substantivised form of the adjective <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*mennisk</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">human, humanlike</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*manniskaz</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_4">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:mens.html>mens</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:mensen.html>mensen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:mensje.html>mensje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>human, any member of the species <i><a href = vnd.unilang:homo.html>Homo</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:sapiens.html>sapiens</a></i>
<dl><dd><i><a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>De</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:mens.html>mens</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> nature <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:politiek.html>politiek</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dier.html>dier</a>.</i>
<dl><dd><i><b><a href = vnd.unilang:man.html>Man</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> by nature a political animal.</i></dd></dl></dd>
<dd><i><a href = vnd.unilang:ik.html>Ik</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ben.html>ben</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ook.html>ook</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:maar.html>maar</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:mens.html>mens</a></b>!</i>

<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:mens.html>mens</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">human</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-heid</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:mensheid.html>mensheid</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>uncountable</i>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="Latn" lang="en">humanity</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en">mankind</span> <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">totality of humans, all members of the genus <i><a href = vnd.unilang:homo.html>Homo</a></i></span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span>

<ol><li><span class="Latn" lang="en">menstruation</span></li></ol>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Zelfstandig_naamwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:zelfstandig.html>Zelfstandig</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naamwoord.html>naamwoord</a></i></span></h4>

***meren.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:meren.html>meren</a> (14331)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:meren.html>meren</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*mēron</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*mairōną</i>, related to <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*maida-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">post</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*mēyt-</i>, <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*meyt-</i>, from <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*mēy-</i>, <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*mey-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:steken.html>stake</a>, pole</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">moor</i>.
</p>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:merken.html>merken</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt"><a href = vnd.unilang:merken.html>merken</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*markijaną</i>.

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:merkwaardig.html>merkwaardig</a> (11253)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:merken.html>merken</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to mark, to notice</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-waardig</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">-able</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">literally</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> remarkable, notable</li>

***merman.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:merman.html>merman</a> (103065)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_English" class="extiw" title="w:Middle English">Middle English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm">mereman</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_English" class="extiw" title="w:Old English">Old English</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ang">*meremann</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:merman.html>merman</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> (suggested by <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_English" class="extiw" title="w:Old English">Old English</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ang">meremenn</i>, <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ang">meremennen</i>, <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ang">meremenin</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">mermaid, siren</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">mer-</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:man.html>man</a></i>. Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Dutch_language" class="extiw" title="w:Dutch language">Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:meerman.html>meerman</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:merman.html>merman</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Meermann</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:merman.html>merman</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:merman.html>merman</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">mermen</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>A legendary creature, human male from the waist up, fishlike from the waist down.
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1653</b>,  <cite>The <a href = vnd.unilang:loves.html>Loves</a> of Hero and Leander: A Mock Poem</cite>, London, page 19:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">The <b><a href = vnd.unilang:meer.html>meer</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:man.html>man</a></b> hath no <a href = vnd.unilang:feet.html>feet</a> but <a href = vnd.unilang:fins.html>fins</a> / And this hath <a href = vnd.unilang:legs.html>legs</a> you see and <a href = vnd.unilang:shins.html>shins</a>.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="en">merguy</span></li></ul>
</body>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:merrie.html>merrie</a> (12075)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:merrie.html>merrie</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*meria</i> (compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_High_German" class="extiw" title="w:Old High German">Old High German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="goh">meriha</i>), from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*marhijō</i>. Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/West_Frisian_language" class="extiw" title="w:West Frisian language">West Frisian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fy">merje</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Mähre</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">mare</i>.

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:mes.html>mes</a> (1464)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_6">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:mets.html>mets</a></i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:mes.html>mes</a></i>, contraction of <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">*metses</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*metisas</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*metsas</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*matisahsą</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">food knife</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, an early compound of <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*matiz</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">food</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*sahsą</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">knife</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>

***mesjogge.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:mesjogge.html>mesjogge</a> (45085)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Yiddish" class="extiw" title="w:Yiddish">Yiddish</a></span> <i class="Hebr mention" lang="yi">משוגע</i> |  <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="yi-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">meshuge</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">crazy</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, derived from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Hebrew_language" class="extiw" title="w:Hebrew language">Hebrew</a></span> <i class="Hebr mention" lang="he">מְשֻׁגָּע</i> |  <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="he-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">meshuge</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">crazy</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:mesjogge.html>mesjogge</a></strong> (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:mesjogge.html>mesjogger</a></b>, <i>superlative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:meest.html>meest</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:mesjogge.html>mesjogge</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl">mesjoggest</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>crazy, insane</li></ol>

***mest.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:mest.html>mest</a> (12997)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:mest.html>mest</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*<a href = vnd.unilang:mist.html>mist</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*mihstuz</i>. Probably derived from <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*mīganą</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to urinate</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*-þuz</i>.
</p><p>Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de"><a href = vnd.unilang:mist.html>Mist</a></i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Gothic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Gothic language">Gothic</a></span> <i class="Goth mention" lang="got">𐌼𐌰𐌹𐌷𐍃𐍄𐌿𐍃</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="got-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">maihstus</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:mest.html>mest</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> or <abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span> (<i>uncountable</i>)
</p>
<ol><li>dung</li>
<li>fertilizer</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><i><a href = vnd.unilang:mest.html>Mest</a></i> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> in modern usage masculine in the Netherlands, but may also be neuter in Belgium.

***met.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:met.html>met</a> (25)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1_2">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">mit</i>, variant of *<i>midi</i> (from which <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:mee.html>mee</a></i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:mede.html>mede</a></i>), from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*midi</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Preposition_4">Preposition</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:met.html>met</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li>with, along with <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">another person</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li>
<li>with, using <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">a tool, instrument or other means</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li>
<li>at, for, during (a holiday/festivity)
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:heb.html>Heb</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:je.html>je</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zin.html>zin</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:om.html>om</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:met.html>met</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:kerst.html>kerst</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:bij.html>bij</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ons.html>ons</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:langs.html>langs</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:te.html>te</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:komen.html>komen</a>?</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">Do you fancy visiting us <b>for</b> Christmas?</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:met.html>met</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*matją</i>, whence also <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Mett</i> (through Low German). Related with Proto-Germanic <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*matiz</i>, whence English <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">meat</i>.
</p>

***metaal.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:metaal.html>metaal</a> (4899)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_French" class="extiw" title="w:Old French">Old French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro">metal</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">metal</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">metallum</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">metal, mine, quarry, mineral</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Ancient Greek">Ancient Greek</a></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">μέταλλον</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">métallon</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">mine, quarry, metal</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">μέταλλευειν</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">métalleuein</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to mine, quarry</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, of unknown origin, but apparently related to <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">μέταλλαν</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">métallan</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to seek after</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, also of unknown origin.
</p>

***metafysica.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:metafysica.html>metafysica</a> (60085)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">metaphysica</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Medieval_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Medieval Greek">Byzantine Greek</a></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">μεταφυσικά</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">metaphusiká</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from the title of the collection by Aristotle <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">μετὰ τὰ φυσικά</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">metà tà phusiká</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, a collection that <a href = vnd.unilang:comes.html>comes</a> after (<i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">μετά</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">metá</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>) Aristotle's collection entitled <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">τὰ φυσικά</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">tà phusiká</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">φυσικός</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">phusikós</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">natural</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">meta-</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:fysica.html>fysica</a></i>.

***meteoor.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:meteoor.html>meteoor</a> (17156)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">meteorum</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Ancient Greek">Ancient Greek</a></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">μετέωρον</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">metéōron</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">μετέωρος</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">metéōros</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">raised from the ground, hanging, lofty</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">μετά</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">metá</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">in the midst of, among, between</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> (English <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">meta</i>) + <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">ἀείρω</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">aeírō</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to <a href = vnd.unilang:lift.html>lift</a>, to heave, to raise up</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p><p>Original sense of “atmospheric phenomenon” <a href = vnd.unilang:gave.html>gave</a> rise to <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">meteorology</i>, now restricted to extraterrestrial <a href = vnd.unilang:objects.html>objects</a> burning up as they enter the atmosphere.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:meteoor.html>meteoor</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:meteoren.html>meteoren</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:meteoor.html>meteoortje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="Latn" lang="en">meteor</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">obsolete</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <span class="Latn" lang="en">luminary</span> <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">light-emitting celestial object</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonym:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl">hemellicht</span></span></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:vallende.html>vallende</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ster.html>ster</a></span></li></ul>

<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Zelfstandig_naamwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:zelfstandig.html>Zelfstandig</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naamwoord.html>naamwoord</a></i></span></h4>
